	<div class="content">
		<article class="article-container article--post ">
			<header class="article__header ">
	<div class="article__title-wrapper">
						<h1 class="article__title">X is launching two new subscription tiers, including a &#8216;Premium+&#8217; ad-free plan</h1>
		</div>

			<div class="article__byline-wrapper">
			
<div class="article__byline">
			<a href="https://techcrunch.com/author/aisha-malik/">
			Aisha Malik		</a>
		<span class="article__byline__meta">
						3 months		</span>
	</div>
		</div>
	
			<div class="article__featured-image-wrapper breakout">
			<img src="https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/twitter-x-logo-musk-2.jpg?w=711" class="article__featured-image" />
		</div>
	</header>

			<div class="article-content">
				<p id="speakable-summary">X, formerly known as Twitter, is introducing <a href="https://twitter.com/premium/status/1717977644996644948" target="_blank" rel="noopener">two new tiers</a> for its subscription offering in order to bring in additional revenue. The social media giant is adding a new Premium+ tier that costs $16 per month and offers the &#8220;largest reply boost&#8221; and removes ads from the For You and Following feeds. The tier also comes with revenue-sharing, along with access to other creator tools.</p>
<p>The second tier launching today is called &#8220;Basic&#8221; and costs $3 per month. The tier doesn&#8217;t come with a blue checkmark, but includes basic features like the ability to edit posts and post longer text and videos. It also offers a &#8220;small reply boost.&#8221;</p>
<div class="embed breakout embed-oembed embed--twitter">
<blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-width="550" data-dnt="true">
<p lang="en" dir="ltr">introducing Premium+</p>
<p>– no ads in For You or Following<br />– largest boost for your replies (vs other Premium tiers or unverified users)<br />– access to our full suite of creator tools</p>
<p>now available on Web ✌️ </p>
<p>subscribe here → <a href="https://t.co/Ywvyijo9CQ">https://t.co/Ywvyijo9CQ</a></p>
<p>&mdash; Premium (@premium) <a href="https://twitter.com/premium/status/1717977644996644948?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">October 27, 2023</a></p></blockquote><div class="piano-inline-promo"></div>
<p></div>
<p>Both of the new tiers are now available on the web.</p>
<p>The new tiers join the standard X Premium tier, which replaced Twitter Blue. The tier costs $8 per month and gives users a blue checkmark, prioritized ranking in replies, bookmark folders, longer posts, text formatting, themes, sms two-factor authentication, encrypted DMs and more.</p>
<p>The launch of the new tiers comes<a href="https://techcrunch.com/2023/10/06/x-to-test-three-tiers-of-its-premium-service-ceo-says-code-shows-one-tier-may-be-ad-free/"> a few weeks</a> after <a href="https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2023-10-05/x-tells-bankers-that-advertisers-are-back-but-spending-less?sref=gni836kR" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Bloomberg</a> reported that X was working on new subscription tiers.</p>
<p>The introduction of the new tiers will give X additional ways to grow revenues as it deals with the loss in advertising dollars that it has faced since Elon Musk took the reins of the platform last fall. Musk&#8217;s controversial changes have turned away advertisers, as major companies ended up pulling their ads from the social network after their ads were displayed next to hate speech <a href="https://fortune.com/2023/08/17/twitter-x-ads-pro-nazi-account-right-wing-hate-groups/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-mrf-link="https://fortune.com/2023/08/17/twitter-x-ads-pro-nazi-account-right-wing-hate-groups/">and pro-Nazi content.</a> Earlier this month, <a href="https://www.reuters.com/technology/us-ad-revenue-musks-x-declined-each-month-since-takeover-data-2023-10-04/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-mrf-link="https://www.reuters.com/technology/us-ad-revenue-musks-x-declined-each-month-since-takeover-data-2023-10-04/">Reuters</a> reported that the company&#8217;s U.S. ad revenue has declined every month since Musk took over, with the latest figures showing a 60% year-over-year decline as of August.</p>
<p>Since taking over the company last year, Musk has been looking for ways to generate additional revenue, and has gone so far as charging users in New Zealand and the Philippines <a href="https://techcrunch.com/2023/10/17/x-starts-experimenting-with-a-1-per-year-fee-for-new-users">$1 per year</a> in order to access the social network.</p>
<div class="embed breakout embed-oembed embed--techcrunch">
<blockquote class="wp-embedded-content" data-secret="w3xp4u7QHX"><p><a href="https://techcrunch.com/2023/10/27/a-year-after-musks-takeover-x-says-an-average-user-spends-32-minutes-per-day-on-the-platform/">A year after Musk&#8217;s takeover, X says an average user spends 32 minutes per day on the platform</a></p></blockquote>
<p></div>
			</div>

\/18\/netflix-confirms-it-wont-have-a-dedicated-app-for-the-apple-vision-pro\/","title":{"rendered":"Netflix confirms it won\u2019t have a dedicated app for the Apple Vision Pro"},"content":{"rendered":"<p id=\"speakable-summary\">Netflix isn\u2019t planning on releasing a dedicated app for the <a href=\"https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/2024\/01\/17\/i-spent-the-morning-with-the-apple-vision-pro\/\">Apple Vision Pro<\/a>, nor will the company modify its iPad version to run on the headset. Instead, users will have to resort to the web version, meaning they can\u2019t access features like downloading titles for offline viewing.<\/p>\n<p>\u201cOur members will be able to enjoy Netflix on the web browser on the Vision Pro, similar to how our members can enjoy Netflix on Macs,\u201d a Netflix spokesperson said in a statement provided to TechCrunch.<\/p>\n<p><a href=\"https:\/\/www.bloomberg.com\/news\/newsletters\/2023-07-23\/apple-vision-pro-will-developers-sell-visionos-apps-for-the-3-499-device-lkfg5b1l\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Bloomberg<\/a> reported in July that Netflix had no plans for a native app, however, this is the official confirmation from the streaming giant.<\/p>\n<p>While the browser version should perform about the same as the iPad version, it\u2019s a letdown for subscribers who were looking forward to having an immersive experience while watching their favorite Netflix content. In comparison, Disney+ appears to want to outshine its rival with four backdrops inspired by Marvel\u2019s Avengers Tower, the Scare Floor from Pixar\u2019s \u201cMonsters Inc.,\u201d the El Capitan Theatre in Hollywood and a Star Wars-inspired environment featuring the cockpit of Luke Skywalker\u2019s landspeeder and the planet Tatooine.<\/p>\n<p>If we look at Netflix\u2019s outdated Meta Quest app, it\u2019s not hard to tell that the streamer maybe isn\u2019t as invested in mixed reality headsets as other companies. Many Quest users have <a href=\"https:\/\/www.meta.com\/experiences\/2184912004923042\/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">complained<\/a> about the app\u2019s \u201cawful resolution,\u201d bugs and overall poor quality.<\/p>\n<p>One user wrote:<\/p>\n<p><div id=\"attachment_2654179\" style=\"width: 593px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><a href=\"https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/01\/Netflix-Quest-app-review.png\"><img fetchpriority=\"high\" decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-2654179\" class=\"size-full wp-image-2654179\" src=\"https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/01\/Netflix-Quest-app-review.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"583\" height=\"375\" srcset=\"https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/01\/Netflix-Quest-app-review.png 583w, https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/01\/Netflix-Quest-app-review.png?resize=150,96 150w, https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/01\/Netflix-Quest-app-review.png?resize=300,193 300w, https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/01\/Netflix-Quest-app-review.png?resize=50,32 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 583px) 100vw, 583px\" \/><\/a><p id=\"caption-attachment-2654179\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"><strong>Image Credits:<\/strong> Meta Quest Store<\/p><\/div><\/p><div class=\"piano-inline-promo\"><\/div>\n<p>Mixed reality headsets are still niche products and Netflix likely believes the Vision Pro won\u2019t be a huge hit with customers \u2013 at least not right away &#8212; especially given the outrageous price point ($3,500).<\/p>\n<p>The Apple Vision Pro will be available for purchase on <a href=\"https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/2024\/01\/08\/apple-vision-pro-goes-on-sale-feb-2\/\">February 2<\/a> and will include the ability to <a href=\"https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/2024\/01\/16\/apple-vision-pro-to-launch-with-150-3d-movies-immersive-films-and-series-disney-max-and-more\/\">download and stream movies and TV shows from popular services<\/a> like Disney+, Apple TV+, Max, Discovery+, Paramount+, Prime Video, Peacock, Pluto TV and Tubi, among others. There will also be 150 3D movies available to rent and purchase, including \u201cAvatar: The Way of Water,\u201d \u201cSpider-Man: Into the Spider-Verse,\u201d \u201cThe Super Mario Bros,\u201d \u201cDune\u201d and more. Preorders for the device open tomorrow, January 19, at 8 a.m. ET.<\/p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout embed-oembed embed--techcrunch\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"745RebyUUz\"><p><a href=\"https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/2024\/01\/16\/apple-vision-pro-to-launch-with-150-3d-movies-immersive-films-and-series-disney-max-and-more\/\">Apple Vision Pro to launch with 150 3D movies, immersive films and series, Disney+, Max and more<\/a><\/p><\/blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" style=\"position: absolute; clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);\" title=\"&#8220;Apple Vision Pro to launch with 150 3D movies, immersive films and series, Disney+, Max and more&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https:\/\/techcrunch.com\/2024\/01\/16\/apple-vision-pro-to-launch-with-150-3d-movies-immersive-films-and-series-disney-max-and-more\/embed\/#?secret=usknzBPbX0#?secret=745RebyUUz\" data-secret=\"745RebyUUz\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"><\/iframe><\/div>\n","protected":false},"excerpt":{"rendered":"<p>Netflix isn\u2019t planning on releasing a dedicated app for the Apple Vision Pro, nor will the company modify its iPad version to run on the headset. /welcome-back-to-the-unicorn-club-10-years-later\/","title":{"rendered":"Welcome
